# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Hockey grips are made with a mean of    and a standard deviation

Given that 10% have a length less than 130cm and 5% have a length greater than 150cm

20 grips are chosen at random, fin the probability that at least 4 of them are above 145cm in length ^9iQWGAPX
